<p><b>Antoine Griezmann</b> (<small>French pronunciation:&#160;&#8203;</small><span title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)" class="IPA"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/French" title="Help:IPA/French">[twan ijzman]</a></span>;<sup id="cite_ref-Griezmann_pronounciation_4-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Griezmann_pronounciation-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup> born 21 March 1991) is a French professional <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">footballer</a> who plays as a <a href="/wiki/Forward_(association_football)" title="Forward (association football)">forward</a> for Spanish club <a href="/wiki/FC_Barcelona" title="FC Barcelona">Barcelona</a> and the <a href="/wiki/France_national_football_team" title="France national football team">French national team</a>.
</p><p>Born and raised in <a href="/wiki/M%C3%A2con" title="Mâcon">Mâcon</a>, Griezmann began his senior career with <a href="/wiki/Real_Sociedad" title="Real Sociedad">Real Sociedad</a> in 2009, with whom he won the <a href="/wiki/Segunda_Divisi%C3%B3n" title="Segunda División">Segunda División</a> title in his <a href="/wiki/2009%E2%80%9310_Segunda_Divisi%C3%B3n" title="200910 Segunda División">first season</a>. In 2014, he joined <a href="/wiki/Atl%C3%A9tico_Madrid" title="Atlético Madrid">Atlético Madrid</a> for a then-club record 30&#160;million, where he broke the club's scoring record for a debut season and was named in the <a href="/wiki/La_Liga_Awards#Other_La_Liga_honours" title="La Liga Awards">201415 La Liga Team of the Season</a>. He was voted <a href="/wiki/La_Liga_Awards#Winners" title="La Liga Awards">La Liga Best Player</a> in 2016, and finished third for the <a href="/wiki/2016_Ballon_d%27Or" title="2016 Ballon d&#39;Or">2016 Ballon d'Or</a> and <a href="/wiki/The_Best_FIFA_Men%27s_Player" title="The Best FIFA Men&#39;s Player">2016 Best FIFA Men's Player</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-theguardian.com_5-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-theguardian.com-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> He finished third and sixth respectively for the awards in 2018,<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> as he helped Atlético Madrid win the <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_UEFA_Europa_League" title="201718 UEFA Europa League">UEFA Europa League</a>, scoring twice in the <a href="/wiki/2018_UEFA_Europa_League_Final" title="2018 UEFA Europa League Final">final</a>. Griezmann also won the <a href="/wiki/2014_Supercopa_de_Espa%C3%B1a" title="2014 Supercopa de España">2014 Supercopa de España</a> and <a href="/wiki/2018_UEFA_Super_Cup" title="2018 UEFA Super Cup">2018 UEFA Super Cup</a>, and ranks as the club's <a href="/wiki/Atl%C3%A9tico_Madrid#Notable_players" title="Atlético Madrid">fifth-highest</a> goalscorer.<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> In 2019, Griezmann signed for league rivals Barcelona in a transfer worth 120&#160;million, becoming the <a href="/wiki/List_of_most_expensive_association_football_transfers#Highest_fees" title="List of most expensive association football transfers">joint-fourth most expensive</a> footballer ever.<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>At international level, Griezmann won the <a href="/wiki/2010_UEFA_European_Under-19_Championship" title="2010 UEFA European Under-19 Championship">2010 UEFA European Under-19 Championship</a>, and made his senior debut for France in 2014, at age 23, and has appeared in four major tournaments. He finished as <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2016#Awards" title="UEFA Euro 2016">top goalscorer</a> and voted as Player of the Tournament as France finished runner-up at <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2016" title="UEFA Euro 2016">UEFA Euro 2016</a>. Griezmann won the <a href="/wiki/FIFA_World_Cup_awards#Golden_Boot" title="FIFA World Cup awards">Silver Boot</a> as the second highest goalscorer at the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018 FIFA World Cup</a> as France won the tournament. He also won the <a href="/wiki/FIFA_World_Cup_awards#Golden_Ball" title="FIFA World Cup awards">Bronze Ball</a> as the third best player, and was named Man of the Match after scoring twice in the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_Final" title="2018 FIFA World Cup Final">final</a>.
</p>
<div id="toc" class="toc" role="navigation" aria-labelledby="mw-toc-heading"><input type="checkbox" role="button" id="toctogglecheckbox" class="toctogglecheckbox" style="display:none" /><div class="toctitle" lang="en" dir="ltr"><h2 id="mw-toc-heading">Contents</h2><span class="toctogglespan"><label class="toctogglelabel" for="toctogglecheckbox"></label></span></div>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_life">Early life</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Antoine_Griezmann&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Early life">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="quotebox pullquote floatright" style="width:27%; ;"><style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r1012376600">.mw-parser-output .quotebox{background-color:#F9F9F9;border:1px solid #aaa;box-sizing:border-box;padding:10px;font-size:88%;max-width:100%}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatleft{margin:0.5em 1.4em 0.8em 0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatright{margin:0.5em 0 0.8em 1.4em}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.centered{margin:0.5em auto 0.8em auto}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatleft p,.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatright p{font-style:inherit}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-title{background-color:#F9F9F9;text-align:center;font-size:larger;font-weight:bold}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-quote.quoted:before{font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:large;color:gray;content:"  ";vertical-align:-45%;line-height:0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-quote.quoted:after{font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:large;color:gray;content:"  ";line-height:0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .left-aligned{text-align:left}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .right-aligned{text-align:right}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .center-aligned{text-align:center}.mw-parser-output .quotebox cite{display:block;font-style:normal}@media screen and (max-width:640px){.mw-parser-output .quotebox{width:100%!important;margin:0 0 0.8em!important;float:none!important}}</style>
<div class="quotebox-quote left-aligned" style="">"I liked [Beckham] a lot. He was my idol. That's why I wear a long-sleeved jersey and wear the No.7. He had a lot of class on and off the pitch. That's what I liked about him. No one had the right foot he had."</div>
<p><cite class="left-aligned" style="">Griezmann on his idol growing up, <a href="/wiki/David_Beckham" title="David Beckham">David Beckham</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup></cite>
</p>
</div>
<p>Griezmann was born in the <a href="/wiki/Communes_of_France" title="Communes of France">commune</a> of <a href="/wiki/M%C3%A2con" title="Mâcon">Mâcon</a> in the département of <a href="/wiki/Sa%C3%B4ne-et-Loire" title="Saône-et-Loire">Saône-et-Loire</a>. His father Alain, a town councillor,<sup id="cite_ref-mais_10-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-mais-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> is of a family who originated from <a href="/wiki/M%C3%BCnster,_Hesse" title="Münster, Hesse">Münster</a>, Germany,<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> hence the Germanic surname.<sup id="cite_ref-wallace_12-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-wallace-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> His surname was originally spelled as "Griesmann", before changing to "Griezmann" for social purposes.<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> His mother Isabelle, a former hospital staff supervising the cleaning team, is of Portuguese descent, and her father Amaro Lopes was a Portuguese footballer for <a href="/wiki/F.C._Pa%C3%A7os_de_Ferreira" title="F.C. Paços de Ferreira">Paços de Ferreira</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-mais_10-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-mais-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> Amaro Lopes came to France with his wife Carolina to work in construction in 1957, where Isabelle was born, and died in 1992 when his grandson was an infant.<sup id="cite_ref-mais_10-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-mais-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> As a child, Griezmann often spent his holidays in <a href="/wiki/Pa%C3%A7os_de_Ferreira" title="Paços de Ferreira">Paços de Ferreira</a>, Portugal.<sup id="cite_ref-mais_10-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-mais-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Griezmann had begun his career playing for hometown club <a href="/w/index.php?title=UF_M%C3%A2connais&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="UF Mâconnais (page does not exist)">Mâcon</a><span class="noprint" style="font-size:85%; font-style: normal;">&#160;&#91;<a href="https://fr.wikipedia.org/wiki/Union_du_Football_m%C3%A2connais" class="extiw" title="fr:Union du Football mâconnais">fr</a>&#93;</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-griezmann_career_14-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-griezmann_career-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> While there, he embarked on several trials with professional clubs in order to earn a spot in one of their youth academies, but was rejected because clubs questioned his size and lightweight frame.<sup id="cite_ref-griezmann_career_14-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-griezmann_career-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> In 2005, while on trial with <a href="/wiki/Montpellier_HSC" title="Montpellier HSC">Montpellier</a>, Griezmann played in a friendly match against the <a href="/wiki/Camp_des_Loges" title="Camp des Loges">youth academy</a> of <a href="/wiki/Paris_Saint-Germain_F.C." title="Paris Saint-Germain F.C.">Paris Saint-Germain</a> in Paris, and impressed several clubs, notably Spanish club <a href="/wiki/Real_Sociedad" title="Real Sociedad">Real Sociedad</a>, whose scouts were attending the event. Following the match, the club's officials offered Griezmann a one-week trial in <a href="/wiki/San_Sebasti%C3%A1n" title="San Sebastián">San Sebastián</a>, which he accepted. He was later offered a second-week stay at the club. The club then contacted his parents and formally offered the player a youth contract. Griezmann's parents were initially reluctant to have their son move to Spain, but allowed him to make the move after positive reassurances.<sup id="cite_ref-griezmann_career_14-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-griezmann_career-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> Because Griezmann spent time at youth level in a Basque club, he is potentially <a href="/wiki/Athletic_Bilbao_signing_policy#Griezmann_debate" title="Athletic Bilbao signing policy">available to play for</a> <a href="/wiki/Athletic_Bilbao" title="Athletic Bilbao">Athletic Bilbao</a>, in spite of being born and growing up in the non-Basque areas of France.<sup id="cite_ref-impossible_16-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-impossible-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Club_career">Club career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Antoine_Griezmann&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Club career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Real_Sociedad">Real Sociedad</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Antoine_Griezmann&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Real Sociedad">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_career">Early career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Antoine_Griezmann&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Early career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>When he first arrived at Real Sociedad, Griezmann lodged with the club's French scout while attending school across the border in <a href="/wiki/Bayonne" title="Bayonne">Bayonne</a>, training in the evenings at the <a href="/wiki/Zubieta_Facilities" title="Zubieta Facilities">club's headquarters</a> in San Sebastián.<sup id="cite_ref-griezmann_career_14-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-griezmann_career-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> It took him time to break into Real Sociedad's first team, but after four years in the <a href="/wiki/Real_Sociedad_Juvenil" class="mw-redirect" title="Real Sociedad Juvenil">club's youth system</a> he made his debut, called up by <a href="/wiki/Mart%C3%ADn_Lasarte" title="Martín Lasarte">Martín Lasarte</a> for Real Sociedad's <a href="/wiki/2009%E2%80%9310_Segunda_Divisi%C3%B3n" title="200910 Segunda División">200910</a> pre-season campaign. In the pre-season, he scored five goals in four appearances and an injury to the team's regular left-winger led to Lasarte selecting him for the start of the season (unusually for a youth graduate, bypassing <a href="/wiki/Real_Sociedad_B" title="Real Sociedad B">the reserve team</a> altogether).<sup id="cite_ref-griezmann_career_14-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-griezmann_career-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2009.E2.80.9311:_Development_and_breakthrough"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="200911:_Development_and_breakthrough">200911: Development and breakthrough</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Antoine_Griezmann&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: 200911: Development and breakthrough">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Griezmann-Helm%C3%A1ntico.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Griezmann-Helm%C3%A1ntico.jpg/170px-Griezmann-Helm%C3%A1ntico.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="172" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Griezmann-Helm%C3%A1ntico.jpg/255px-Griezmann-Helm%C3%A1ntico.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Griezmann-Helm%C3%A1ntico.jpg/340px-Griezmann-Helm%C3%A1ntico.jpg 2x" data-file-width="927" data-file-height="939" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Griezmann-Helm%C3%A1ntico.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Griezmann, aged 18, playing for Real Sociedad against <a href="/wiki/UD_Salamanca" title="UD Salamanca">UD Salamanca</a> in March 2010</div></div></div>
<p>On 2 September 2009, Griezmann made his competitive debut in the team's <a href="/wiki/2009%E2%80%9310_Copa_del_Rey" title="200910 Copa del Rey">Copa del Rey</a> match against <a href="/wiki/Rayo_Vallecano" title="Rayo Vallecano">Rayo Vallecano</a> appearing as a <a href="/wiki/Substitute_(association_football)" title="Substitute (association football)">substitute</a> in the 77th minute of a 20 defeat.<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> Four days later, he made his league debut appearing as a substitute against <a href="/wiki/Real_Murcia" title="Real Murcia">Real Murcia</a>. On 27 September, he made his first professional start and also scored his first professional goal against <a href="/wiki/SD_Huesca" title="SD Huesca">Huesca</a> in a 20 win.<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> Two weeks later, Griezmann scored his second goal of the campaign in a 20 win over <a href="/wiki/UD_Salamanca" title="UD Salamanca">Salamanca</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> In November 2009, he scored goals in back-to-back matches against <a href="/wiki/H%C3%A9rcules_CF" title="Hércules CF">Hércules</a> and <a href="/wiki/Recreativo_de_Huelva" title="Recreativo de Huelva">Recreativo de Huelva</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> The goal against the latter club was the only goal of the match.<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> Griezmann appeared consistently in the team for the rest of the season, scoring two more goals in wins over <a href="/wiki/C%C3%A1diz_CF" title="Cádiz CF">Cádiz</a> and <a href="/wiki/CD_Numancia" title="CD Numancia">Numancia</a> as Real Sociedad earned promotion to <a href="/wiki/La_Liga" title="La Liga">La Liga</a> for the <a href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%9311_La_Liga" title="201011 La Liga">201011 season</a> as league winners.<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 8 April 2010, Griezmann signed his first professional contract agreeing to a five-year deal with the club until 2015 with a release clause of 30&#160;million.<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> Prior to signing the contract, he drew considerable interest from <a href="/wiki/Ligue_1" title="Ligue 1">Ligue 1</a> clubs <a href="/wiki/Olympique_Lyonnais" title="Olympique Lyonnais">Lyon</a>, <a href="/wiki/AS_Saint-%C3%89tienne" title="AS Saint-Étienne">Saint-Étienne</a> and <a href="/wiki/AJ_Auxerre" title="AJ Auxerre">Auxerre</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Antoine_Griezmann_2012_Levante.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5a/Antoine_Griezmann_2012_Levante.jpg/170px-Antoine_Griezmann_2012_Levante.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="295" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5a/Antoine_Griezmann_2012_Levante.jpg/255px-Antoine_Griezmann_2012_Levante.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/5/5a/Antoine_Griezmann_2012_Levante.jpg 2x" data-file-width="303" data-file-height="525" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Antoine_Griezmann_2012_Levante.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Griezmann playing for Real Sociedad in 2012</div></div></div>
<p>Griezmann made his debut in the Spanish first division on 29 August 2010, in the season's first match. In a post-game interview, he described the occasion as "fulfilling his childhood dream".<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup> In the team's first match after the September international break, Griezmann assisted on the equalising goal scored by <a href="/wiki/Ra%C3%BAl_Tamudo" title="Raúl Tamudo">Raúl Tamudo</a> against <a href="/wiki/Real_Madrid_C.F." class="mw-redirect" title="Real Madrid C.F.">Real Madrid</a>. Madrid later won the match 21 following a goal from <a href="/wiki/Cristiano_Ronaldo" title="Cristiano Ronaldo">Cristiano Ronaldo</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> On 25 October, Griezmann scored his first goal in the league in a 30 victory over <a href="/wiki/Deportivo_de_La_Coru%C3%B1a" title="Deportivo de La Coruña">Deportivo de La Coruña</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> He celebrated the goal by pretending to drive a truck that was parked near the field.<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> A week later, Griezmann scored the opening goal in a 21 win over <a href="/wiki/M%C3%A1laga_CF" title="Málaga CF">Málaga</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup> In November 2010, Griezmann scored the only goal in the team's 21 loss to Hércules.<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup> In the team's second match of the new year, he netted the second goal in the team's 40 victory over <a href="/wiki/Getafe_CF" title="Getafe CF">Getafe</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> After going scoreless in the next nine matches, Griezmann returned to his scoring form in March netting the only goal for <i>Txuri-urdin</i> in the team's 21 defeat to <a href="/wiki/Racing_de_Santander" title="Racing de Santander">Racing Santander</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2011.E2.80.9314:_Individual_success"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201114:_Individual_success">201114: Individual success</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Antoine_Griezmann&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: 201114: Individual success">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>After sitting out the first league match of the <a href="/wiki/2011%E2%80%9312_La_Liga" title="201112 La Liga">201112 campaign</a>, in Griezmann's first competitive match of the season against the <a href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%9311_La_Liga" title="201011 La Liga">defending champions</a> <a href="/wiki/FC_Barcelona" title="FC Barcelona">Barcelona</a> two weeks later, he scored the equalising goal in a 22 draw.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In the final league game of the <a href="/wiki/2012%E2%80%9313_La_Liga" title="201213 La Liga">201213</a> campaign, he scored the only goal of the game against Deportivo de La Coruña, securing qualification for the <a href="/wiki/2013%E2%80%9314_UEFA_Champions_League" title="201314 UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a> for the first time since <a href="/wiki/2003%E2%80%9304_UEFA_Champions_League" title="200304 UEFA Champions League">200304</a> while also relegating Deportivo.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>At the start of the following season, Griezmann scored a volley against Lyon in his home nation of France which helped Real Sociedad qualify for the Champions League group stage (40 on aggregate).<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> Another important goal was also a volley, this time against <a href="/wiki/Athletic_Bilbao" title="Athletic Bilbao">Athletic Bilbao</a> in a <a href="/wiki/Basque_derby" title="Basque derby">Basque derby</a> league match at <a href="/wiki/Anoeta_Stadium" title="Anoeta Stadium">Anoeta Stadium</a> in January 2014 which ended in a 20 victory for Real.<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="Atl.C3.A9tico_Madrid"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Atlético_Madrid">Atlético Madrid</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Antoine_Griezmann&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Atlético Madrid">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Antoine_Griezmann_-_CdR_-_RM_v_ATL_(edited)_-_1.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e2/Antoine_Griezmann_-_CdR_-_RM_v_ATL_%28edited%29_-_1.jpg/170px-Antoine_Griezmann_-_CdR_-_RM_v_ATL_%28edited%29_-_1.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="216" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e2/Antoine_Griezmann_-_CdR_-_RM_v_ATL_%28edited%29_-_1.jpg/255px-Antoine_Griezmann_-_CdR_-_RM_v_ATL_%28edited%29_-_1.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e2/Antoine_Griezmann_-_CdR_-_RM_v_ATL_%28edited%29_-_1.jpg/340px-Antoine_Griezmann_-_CdR_-_RM_v_ATL_%28edited%29_-_1.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1983" data-file-height="2523" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Antoine_Griezmann_-_CdR_-_RM_v_ATL_(edited)_-_1.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Griezmann playing for <a href="/wiki/Atl%C3%A9tico_Madrid" title="Atlético Madrid">Atlético Madrid</a> in 2015</div></div></div>
<h4><span id="2014.E2.80.9315:_Transfer_and_rise_to_prominence"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201415:_Transfer_and_rise_to_prominence">201415: Transfer and rise to prominence</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Antoine_Griezmann&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: 201415: Transfer and rise to prominence">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>On 28 July 2014, <a href="/wiki/Atl%C3%A9tico_Madrid" title="Atlético Madrid">Atlético Madrid</a> reached an agreement with Real Sociedad for the transfer of Griezmann, for a fee believed to be close to his 30&#160;million (<a href="/wiki/Pound_sterling" title="Pound sterling">£</a>24&#160;million) buy-out clause.<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> He passed the medical examination the same day and signed a six-year contract on 29 July.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Griezmann made his competitive debut in the first leg of the <a href="/wiki/2014_Supercopa_de_Espa%C3%B1a" title="2014 Supercopa de España">2014 Supercopa de España</a> on 19 August, a 11 draw away to Real Madrid, replacing <a href="/wiki/Sa%C3%BAl_%C3%91%C3%ADguez" title="Saúl Ñíguez">Saúl</a> after 57 minutes.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup> On 17 September, he scored his first goal for the club, in a <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">Champions League</a> <a href="/wiki/2014%E2%80%9315_UEFA_Champions_League_group_stage" title="201415 UEFA Champions League group stage">group stage</a> match against <a href="/wiki/Olympiacos_F.C." title="Olympiacos F.C.">Olympiacos</a>, in a game which Atlético eventually lost 32.<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> Griezmann netted a brace in a 42 win over <a href="/wiki/C%C3%B3rdoba_CF" title="Córdoba CF">Córdoba</a> on 1 November, his first league goals for the club.<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup> On 21 December 2014, he scored his first La Liga hat-trick as Atlético won 41 at Athletic Bilbao, having trailed at half-time.<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup> He was the <a href="/wiki/La_Liga_Player_of_the_Month" title="La Liga Player of the Month">La Liga Player of the Month</a> for January 2015 despite appearing in only three of Atlético's five matches.<sup id="cite_ref-lfp_january_49-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-lfp_january-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 7 April 2015, Griezmann scored the second in a 20 home victory over Real Sociedad; out of respect to his formative club, the celebrations were minimal.<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> Two weeks later he scored a brace against <a href="/wiki/Elche_CF" title="Elche CF">Elche</a> in a 30 home win, bringing him to a total of 22 goals in the league season, overtaking <a href="/wiki/Karim_Benzema" title="Karim Benzema">Karim Benzema</a> for the highest total by a French player in a single Spanish top-division campaign.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> He finished the season with 22 goals in 37 games, and was selected as the only Atlético player and one of three forwards in the Team of the Year at the <a href="/wiki/LFP_Awards" class="mw-redirect" title="LFP Awards">LFP Awards</a>, alongside <a href="/wiki/Cristiano_Ronaldo" title="Cristiano Ronaldo">Cristiano Ronaldo</a> and <a href="/wiki/Lionel_Messi" title="Lionel Messi">Lionel Messi</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2015.E2.80.9317:_Ballon_d.27Or_and_FIFA_Best_Player_nominations"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201517:_Ballon_d'Or_and_FIFA_Best_Player_nominations">201517: Ballon d'Or and FIFA Best Player nominations</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Antoine_Griezmann&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: 201517: Ballon d&#039;Or and FIFA Best Player nominations">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>On 22 August 2015, Griezmann scored the only goal as Atlético began the season with a home victory over promoted <a href="/wiki/UD_Las_Palmas" title="UD Las Palmas">Las Palmas</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup> He scored both of the goals on 15 September, as they won at <a href="/wiki/Galatasaray_S.K._(football)" title="Galatasaray S.K. (football)">Galatasaray</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_UEFA_Champions_League_group_stage" title="201516 UEFA Champions League group stage">Champions League group stage</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup> A week later, he repeated the feat to defeat local neighbours Getafe and put Atlético on top of the league.<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> On 18 October, in his return to Real Sociedad, Griezmann chipped goalkeeper <a href="/wiki/Ger%C3%B3nimo_Rulli" title="Gerónimo Rulli">Gerónimo Rulli</a> in the ninth minute of a 20 away win (as in the fixture six months earlier, he did not celebrate the goal).<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 27 February 2016, Griezmann scored the only goal as Atlético won away to Real Madrid.<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup> On 13 April, he scored both goals in a 20 quarter-final second leg win at the <a href="/wiki/Vicente_Calder%C3%B3n_Stadium" title="Vicente Calderón Stadium">Vicente Calderón Stadium</a> that knocked holders Barcelona out of the <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_UEFA_Champions_League" title="201516 UEFA Champions League">Champions League</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> On 3 May, he scored the decisive away goal against <a href="/wiki/FC_Bayern_Munich" title="FC Bayern Munich">Bayern Munich</a> in the semi-final second leg at the <a href="/wiki/Allianz_Arena" title="Allianz Arena">Allianz Arena</a> to send Atlético to the <a href="/wiki/2016_UEFA_Champions_League_Final" title="2016 UEFA Champions League Final">final</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup> Griezmann hit the crossbar with a penalty two minutes into the second half with his team trailing 10 against Real Madrid in the Champions League final at <a href="/wiki/Milan" title="Milan">Milan</a>'s <a href="/wiki/San_Siro" title="San Siro">San Siro</a> on 28 May. He scored in the penalty shootout after the match had ended 11 after extra time, but Atlético ultimately lost 53.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Antoine_Griezmann_September_2017.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/90/Antoine_Griezmann_September_2017.jpg/170px-Antoine_Griezmann_September_2017.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="216" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/90/Antoine_Griezmann_September_2017.jpg/255px-Antoine_Griezmann_September_2017.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/9/90/Antoine_Griezmann_September_2017.jpg 2x" data-file-width="274" data-file-height="348" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Antoine_Griezmann_September_2017.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Griezmann with Atlético Madrid in 2017</div></div></div>
<p>On 23 June 2016, Griezmann signed a new contract with Atlético, which would keep him at the club until 2021.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (August 2019)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup> On 1 November 2016, Griezmann scored both of Atlético's goals (with his second in the 93rd minute) in their 21 home win against <a href="/wiki/FC_Rostov" title="FC Rostov">Rostov</a> in a <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_UEFA_Champions_League_group_stage" title="201617 UEFA Champions League group stage">201617 Champions League</a> Group D match (in which he was voted the Player of the Match) to enable Atlético to progress to the round of 16 with two matches to spare.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> On 22 April 2017, he scored the only goal of a win at <a href="/wiki/RCD_Espanyol" title="RCD Espanyol">RCD Espanyol</a>, thus becoming the second Frenchman after <a href="/wiki/Karim_Benzema" title="Karim Benzema">Karim Benzema</a> to score 100 La Liga goals (in 247 games).<sup id="cite_ref-100th_64-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-100th-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After another trophyless season, and amid speculation that he could leave Atlético for Manchester United after the conclusion of the 201617 season, he extended his contract at the club by one year in June 2017, after learning that Atletico were given a transfer ban and that they could not sign a replacement.<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup> His reported release clause was also raised to 100&#160;million (£87&#160;million).<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (August 2019)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2017.E2.80.9318:_UEFA_Europa_League_win"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201718:_UEFA_Europa_League_win">201718: UEFA Europa League win</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Antoine_Griezmann&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: 201718: UEFA Europa League win">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>On 19 August 2017, Griezmann earned his first red card during a draw against <a href="/wiki/Girona_FC" title="Girona FC">Girona</a> and received a two-match ban. He was initially booked for diving in the penalty box, then his reaction of using foul language toward the referee earned him a second booking.<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup> He was named La Liga Player of the Month for February 2018 after registering eight goals and two assists during the period, including scoring seven in four days (a hat-trick against <a href="/wiki/Sevilla_FC" title="Sevilla FC">Sevilla</a> and four against <a href="/wiki/CD_Legan%C3%A9s" title="CD Leganés">Leganés</a>).<sup id="cite_ref-feb18_68-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-feb18-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup> His second in the 40 win against the latter was his 100th goal for Atlético, becoming only the third player of the 21st century to do so after <a href="/wiki/Sergio_Ag%C3%BCero" title="Sergio Agüero">Sergio Agüero</a> and <a href="/wiki/Fernando_Torres" title="Fernando Torres">Fernando Torres</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He scored in the first leg of the <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_UEFA_Europa_League" title="201718 UEFA Europa League">201718 UEFA Europa League</a> semi-final away to <a href="/wiki/Arsenal_F.C." title="Arsenal F.C.">Arsenal</a> and assisted <a href="/wiki/Diego_Costa" title="Diego Costa">Diego Costa</a> for the only goal in the return, contributing to <i>Atléti'</i>s 21 aggregate victory and progression to the final, held in <a href="/wiki/Lyon" title="Lyon">Lyon</a> and against French opposition in <a href="/wiki/Olympique_de_Marseille" title="Olympique de Marseille">Marseille</a>;<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup> he then scored twice in <a href="/wiki/2018_UEFA_Europa_League_Final" title="2018 UEFA Europa League Final">the final</a> as his club claimed the trophy for the third time in nine years.<sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After months of speculation linking him with a 100 million (£88 million) move to Barcelona, which came after Atlético reported Barcelona to <a href="/wiki/FIFA" title="FIFA">FIFA</a> over an alleged illegal approach for Griezmann in December 2017,<sup id="cite_ref-BBC_Sport_72-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBC_Sport-72">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup> Griezmann signed a contract extension with Atlético on 19 June 2018 until 2023. This came days after he rejected a move to the <a href="/wiki/Camp_Nou" title="Camp Nou">Camp Nou</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-New_contract_74-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-New_contract-74">&#91;74&#93;</a></sup> He wrote a message to Atlético on social media, "My fans, my team, MY HOME!!!" in Spanish, French and English along with a video in which he is seen walking around Madrid.<sup id="cite_ref-New_contract_74-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-New_contract-74">&#91;74&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2018.E2.80.9319:_Final_season_with_Atl.C3.A9tico"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201819:_Final_season_with_Atlético">201819: Final season with Atlético</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Antoine_Griezmann&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: 201819: Final season with Atlético">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>On 15 August, Griezmann started in Atlético's 42 extra-time win over Real Madrid in the <a href="/wiki/2018_UEFA_Super_Cup" title="2018 UEFA Super Cup">2018 UEFA Super Cup</a> in <a href="/wiki/Tallinn" title="Tallinn">Tallinn</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On Matchday 2 of the <a href="/wiki/2018-19_UEFA_Champions_League" class="mw-redirect" title="2018-19 UEFA Champions League">Champions League</a>, Griezmann scored a goal in either half to give his team a 31 home win over Belgian champions <a href="/wiki/Club_Brugge_KV" title="Club Brugge KV">Club Brugge</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup> Later on Matchday 4 he scored Atletico's second goal against German side <a href="/wiki/Borussia_Dortmund" title="Borussia Dortmund">Borussia Dortmund</a> as Atletico Madrid won the reverse fixture at home by a 20 margin following a 40 defeat against the same opponents earlier in the competition at the <a href="/wiki/Westfalenstadion" title="Westfalenstadion">Westfalenstadion</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-77" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-77">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup> In the following game he again scored the second goal in a 20 win against French side <a href="/wiki/AS_Monaco_FC" title="AS Monaco FC">Monaco</a>, to ensure his team's qualification for the <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_UEFA_Champions_League_knockout_phase" title="201819 UEFA Champions League knockout phase">next round</a> of the Champions League.<sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-78">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="quotebox pullquote floatright" style="width:33%; ;"><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1012376600"/>
<div class="quotebox-quote left-aligned" style="">"These five years have been incredible. Thank you very much for everything, I carry you in my heart."</div>
<p><cite class="left-aligned" style="">Griezmann after announcing his departure from Atlético Madrid on 14 May 2019.<sup id="cite_ref-79" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-79">&#91;79&#93;</a></sup></cite>
</p>
</div>
<p>On 15 December, Griezmann played his 300th league contest in the Spanish top division, a game in which he scored twice while setting up another, as Atlético Madrid won 32 away to <a href="/wiki/Real_Valladolid" title="Real Valladolid">Real Valladolid</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-80" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-80">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup> In the following week, he scored his 200th career goal, from the spot in a 10 win over <a href="/wiki/RCD_Espanyol" title="RCD Espanyol">Espanyol</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup> On 26 January, in a league fixture at home against <a href="/wiki/Getafe_CF" title="Getafe CF">Getafe</a>, he scored his 10th league goal of the season in a 20 win as Atlético closed the gap between league leaders Barcelona to just 2 points.<sup id="cite_ref-82" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-82">&#91;82&#93;</a></sup> On 10 February, he scored in a 31 derby defeat against Real Madrid, equalling <a href="/wiki/Fernando_Torres" title="Fernando Torres">Fernando Torres</a>'s record-which he later broke in the following week by scoring the only goal in a 10 win against <a href="/wiki/Rayo_Vallecano" title="Rayo Vallecano">Rayo Vallecano</a>, to become the fifth highest goalscorer in Atlético history with 130 goals.<sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83">&#91;83&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 14 May 2019, Griezmann announced that he would be leaving Atlético Madrid after five seasons, after being heavily linked to Barcelona, who reportedly intended to pay the 120 million buy-out clause set by the club.<sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84">&#91;84&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Barcelona">Barcelona</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Antoine_Griezmann&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Barcelona">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quotebox pullquote floatright" style="width:33%; ;"><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1012376600"/>
<div class="quotebox-quote left-aligned" style="">"I didn't leave Atletico for money [or] to win the Champions League or to win more trophies. I left to learn a new style of play, new philosophies [at] another team".</div>
<p><cite class="left-aligned" style=""> Griezmann on why he joined Barcelona.<sup id="cite_ref-85" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-85">&#91;85&#93;</a></sup></cite>
</p>
</div>
<p>On 12 July 2019, <a href="/wiki/FC_Barcelona" title="FC Barcelona">Barcelona</a> announced the signing of Griezmann after they paid his 120 million buy-out clause, with the player set to sign a five-year contract with the club.<sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86">&#91;86&#93;</a></sup> Later that day, however, <a href="/wiki/Atl%C3%A9tico_Madrid" title="Atlético Madrid">Atlético Madrid</a> disputed Barcelona's deal to sign the player, stating that the fee paid falls 80 million short of his release clause, claiming that Griezmann had agreed to move to the Nou Camp before 1 July, when his 200 million buy-out clause was lowered to 120 million.<sup id="cite_ref-87" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-87">&#91;87&#93;</a></sup> Atlético later stated they have "started the procedures it considers appropriate for the defense of its legitimate rights and interests" as a result of any deal, with reports in Spanish media suggesting the club planned to go to football's governing body <a href="/wiki/FIFA" title="FIFA">FIFA</a> to argue their case.<sup id="cite_ref-88" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-88">&#91;88&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-89" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-89">&#91;89&#93;</a></sup> On 14 July, he was presented at the <a href="/wiki/Camp_Nou" title="Camp Nou">Camp Nou</a> and was handed the number 17 shirt, and made his debut in a pre-season friendly in Japan against <a href="/wiki/Chelsea_F.C." title="Chelsea F.C.">Chelsea</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-90" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-90">&#91;90&#93;</a></sup> On the same day, some Atlético Madrid fans defaced Griezmann's plaque outside the <a href="/wiki/Metropolitano_Stadium" title="Metropolitano Stadium">Wanda Metropolitano</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-91" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-91">&#91;91&#93;</a></sup> as the club officially submitted a complaint to <a href="/wiki/La_Liga" title="La Liga">La Liga</a>, whose president <a href="/wiki/Javier_Tebas" title="Javier Tebas">Javier Tebas</a> later stated "it is possible to block [Griezmann's] transfer", but also noted "La Liga have [yet] to decide [the] course of action".<sup id="cite_ref-BBC_Sport_72-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBC_Sport-72">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup> The transfer was eventually upheld.
</p>
<h4><span id="2019.E2.80.9321:_Debut_season_and_struggles"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201921:_Debut_season_and_struggles">201921: Debut season and struggles</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Antoine_Griezmann&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: 201921: Debut season and struggles">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Griezmann made his competitive debut on 16 August 2019 in a 10 defeat to <a href="/wiki/Athletic_Bilbao" title="Athletic Bilbao">Athletic Bilbao</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-92" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-92">&#91;92&#93;</a></sup> On 25 August, Griezmann scored a brace and assisted during his home debut, which ended in a 52 win against <a href="/wiki/Real_Betis" title="Real Betis">Real Betis</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-93" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-93">&#91;93&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-94" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-94">&#91;94&#93;</a></sup>
After substituting injured <a href="/wiki/Ousmane_Demb%C3%A9l%C3%A9" title="Ousmane Dembélé">Ousmane Dembélé</a> after 26 minutes of the first half, he scored his first <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">Champions League</a> goal for the club on 27 November 2019 in a 31 win against <a href="/wiki/Borussia_Dortmund" title="Borussia Dortmund">Borussia Dortmund</a>, assisted by <a href="/wiki/Lionel_Messi" title="Lionel Messi">Lionel Messi</a>. In their <a href="/wiki/2019%E2%80%9320_Supercopa_de_Espa%C3%B1a" title="201920 Supercopa de España">Supercopa de España</a> match against <a href="/wiki/Atl%C3%A9tico_Madrid" title="Atlético Madrid">Atlético Madrid</a>, Griezmann scored his side's second goal against his former club in an eventual 23 defeat.<sup id="cite_ref-95" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-95">&#91;95&#93;</a></sup> Griezmann became the first player of the season to score in every major competition for Barcelona when he netted a brace in the <a href="/wiki/Copa_del_Rey" title="Copa del Rey">Copa del Rey</a> against <a href="/wiki/UD_Ibiza" title="UD Ibiza">Ibiza</a> in a narrow 21 win.<sup id="cite_ref-96" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-96">&#91;96&#93;</a></sup> On 25 February 2020, Griezmann scored Barcelona's equalizer in their 11 Champions League round of 16 draw against <a href="/wiki/S.S.C._Napoli" title="S.S.C. Napoli">Napoli</a>, becoming the first Barcelona player other than Messi to score a Champions League away goal in the knockout stage since 2015.<sup id="cite_ref-97" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-97">&#91;97&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 1 November 2020, Griezmann scored his first goal of the <a href="/wiki/2020%E2%80%9321_FC_Barcelona_season" title="202021 FC Barcelona season">202021 season</a> in a 11 away draw against <a href="/wiki/Deportivo_Alav%C3%A9s" title="Deportivo Alavés">Alavés</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-98" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-98">&#91;98&#93;</a></sup> On 17 January 2021, Griezmann scored a brace in a 32 loss against <a href="/wiki/Athletic_Bilbao" title="Athletic Bilbao">Athletic Bilbao</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2020%E2%80%9321_Supercopa_de_Espa%C3%B1a_Final" class="mw-redirect" title="202021 Supercopa de España Final">202021 Supercopa de España final</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-99" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-99">&#91;99&#93;</a></sup> On 3 February, Griezmann scored and assisted twice as Barcelona made a comeback after being 20 down until the 88th minute to win 53 at the end of extra-time against <a href="/wiki/Granada_CF" title="Granada CF">Granada</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2020%E2%80%9321_Copa_del_Rey" title="202021 Copa del Rey">quarter-finals</a> of the Copa del Rey.<sup id="cite_ref-100" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-100">&#91;100&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="International_career">International career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Antoine_Griezmann&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: International career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Youth">Youth</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Antoine_Griezmann&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Youth">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Antoine_Griezmann.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0b/Antoine_Griezmann.jpg/170px-Antoine_Griezmann.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="227" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0b/Antoine_Griezmann.jpg/255px-Antoine_Griezmann.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0b/Antoine_Griezmann.jpg/340px-Antoine_Griezmann.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3000" data-file-height="4000" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Antoine_Griezmann.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Griezmann with <a href="/wiki/France_national_under-21_football_team" title="France national under-21 football team">France U21s</a> in 2011</div></div></div>
<p>Due to playing in Spain, Griezmann went unnoticed by several <a href="/wiki/France_national_youth_football_team" title="France national youth football team">France youth international</a> coaches.<sup id="cite_ref-101" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-101">&#91;101&#93;</a></sup> After his success with Real Sociedad, on 23 February 2010, he was named to the <a href="/wiki/France_national_under-19_football_team" title="France national under-19 football team">France under-19 team</a> to play in two <a href="/wiki/Exhibition_game" title="Exhibition game">friendly matches</a> against <a href="/wiki/Ukraine_national_football_team" title="Ukraine national football team">Ukraine</a>. On 2 March, Griezmann made his youth international debut appearing in the team's 00 draw with Ukraine.<sup id="cite_ref-102" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-102">&#91;102&#93;</a></sup> In the return leg two days later, he scored the game-winning goal in the 88th minute to give France a 21 victory.<sup id="cite_ref-103" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-103">&#91;103&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 7 June 2010, Griezmann was named to coach <a href="/wiki/Francis_Smerecki" title="Francis Smerecki">Francis Smerecki</a>'s 18-man squad to participate in the <a href="/wiki/2010_UEFA_European_Under-19_Championship" title="2010 UEFA European Under-19 Championship">2010 UEFA European Under-19 Championship</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-104" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-104">&#91;104&#93;</a></sup> In the tournament, he scored two goals and provided an <a href="/wiki/Assist_(football)" class="mw-redirect" title="Assist (football)">assist</a> in the team's second group stage match against <a href="/wiki/Austria_national_under-19_football_team" title="Austria national under-19 football team">Austria</a>, a 50 win, as the national team eventually won the competition on home soil.<sup id="cite_ref-105" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-105">&#91;105&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-106" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-106">&#91;106&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-107" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-107">&#91;107&#93;</a></sup> He was named in the Team of the Tournament.<sup id="cite_ref-u19_team_108-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-u19_team-108">&#91;108&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Due to France's victory at the UEFA Under-19 championship, the nation qualified for the <a href="/wiki/2011_FIFA_U-20_World_Cup" title="2011 FIFA U-20 World Cup">2011 FIFA U-20 World Cup</a>, which merited <a href="/wiki/France_national_under-20_football_team" title="France national under-20 football team">under-20 team</a> appearances for Griezmann. On 28 September 2010, he was called up to the team to participate in friendly matches against Portugal and the <a href="/wiki/Juventus_F.C._Youth_Sector" title="Juventus F.C. Youth Sector">reserve team</a> of Italian club <a href="/wiki/Juventus_F.C." title="Juventus F.C.">Juventus</a>. Griezmann, however, did not appear in either match due to being sent home early after suffering a thigh injury during a training session.<sup id="cite_ref-109" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-109">&#91;109&#93;</a></sup> The following month, despite still being eligible to appear at under-20 level, he was called up to the <a href="/wiki/France_national_under-21_football_team" title="France national under-21 football team">under-21 team</a> by coach <a href="/wiki/Erick_Mombaerts" title="Erick Mombaerts">Erick Mombaerts</a> as a replacement for the injured <a href="/wiki/Gabriel_Obertan" title="Gabriel Obertan">Gabriel Obertan</a> to play in a friendly match against <a href="/wiki/Russia_national_under-21_football_team" title="Russia national under-21 football team">Russia</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-110" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-110">&#91;110&#93;</a></sup> Griezmann made his under-21 debut in the match appearing as a second-half substitute in a 10 defeat.<sup id="cite_ref-111" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-111">&#91;111&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After appearing in two matches with the under-21 team, Griezmann returned to under-20 level and made his debut with the team on 9 February 2011 in a 21 victory over <a href="/wiki/England_national_under-20_football_team" title="England national under-20 football team">England</a> at the <a href="/wiki/New_Meadow" title="New Meadow">New Meadow</a>, assisting <a href="/wiki/Cl%C3%A9ment_Grenier" title="Clément Grenier">Clément Grenier</a>'s equaliser.<sup id="cite_ref-112" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-112">&#91;112&#93;</a></sup> On 10 June 2011, he was named to the 21-man squad to participate in the U-20 World Cup. He made his debut in the competition on 30 July 2011 in the team's 41 defeat to the hosts <a href="/wiki/Colombia_national_under-20_football_team" title="Colombia national under-20 football team">Colombia</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-113" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-113">&#91;113&#93;</a></sup> On 10 August, in France's Round of 16 match against <a href="/wiki/Ecuador_national_under-20_football_team" title="Ecuador national under-20 football team">Ecuador</a>, Griezmann scored the game-winning goal in a 10 victory.<sup id="cite_ref-114" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-114">&#91;114&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In November 2012, Griezmann was suspended, along with four other youth players, from France's national teams until 31 December 2013 for disciplinary reasons regarding a late night out before training.<sup id="cite_ref-115" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-115">&#91;115&#93;</a></sup> During this time, he considered switching allegiance to his ancestral Portugal.<sup id="cite_ref-mais_10-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-mais-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Senior">Senior</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Antoine_Griezmann&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Senior">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:152px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Antoine_Griezmann_in_2017_(cropped).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3e/Antoine_Griezmann_in_2017_%28cropped%29.jpg/150px-Antoine_Griezmann_in_2017_%28cropped%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="150" height="225" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3e/Antoine_Griezmann_in_2017_%28cropped%29.jpg/225px-Antoine_Griezmann_in_2017_%28cropped%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3e/Antoine_Griezmann_in_2017_%28cropped%29.jpg/300px-Antoine_Griezmann_in_2017_%28cropped%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2735" data-file-height="4098" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Antoine_Griezmann_in_2017_(cropped).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Griezmann (pictured in 2017) made his senior debut for <a href="/wiki/France_national_football_team" title="France national football team">France</a> in 2014</div></div></div>
<p>On 27 February 2014, Griezmann received a call-up to <a href="/wiki/France_national_football_team" title="France national football team">France</a>'s senior squad by coach <a href="/wiki/Didier_Deschamps" title="Didier Deschamps">Didier Deschamps</a> to play in a friendly against the <a href="/wiki/Netherlands_national_football_team" title="Netherlands national football team">Netherlands</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Stade_de_France" title="Stade de France">Stade de France</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-116" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-116">&#91;116&#93;</a></sup> He earned his first cap on 5 March, appearing as a starter in the 20 home win and playing the first 68 minutes.<sup id="cite_ref-117" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-117">&#91;117&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="2014_World_Cup">2014 World Cup</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Antoine_Griezmann&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: 2014 World Cup">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>On 13 May, he was named in Deschamps' squad for the <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2014 FIFA World Cup">2014 FIFA World Cup</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-118" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-118">&#91;118&#93;</a></sup> On 1 June, playing against <a href="/wiki/Paraguay_national_football_team" title="Paraguay national football team">Paraguay</a> in Nice, he scored his first international goal for France, opening a 11 draw. He added two more as a late substitute for <a href="/wiki/Olivier_Giroud" title="Olivier Giroud">Olivier Giroud</a> in France's final warm-up match, against <a href="/wiki/Jamaica_national_football_team" title="Jamaica national football team">Jamaica</a> on 8 June, the final two in an 80 win.<sup id="cite_ref-119" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-119">&#91;119&#93;</a></sup> On 15 June, he was selected to start in France's first match of the World Cup, replacing the injured <a href="/wiki/Franck_Rib%C3%A9ry" title="Franck Ribéry">Franck Ribéry</a> on the left side of <i>Les Bleus'</i> attack as they defeated <a href="/wiki/Honduras_national_football_team" title="Honduras national football team">Honduras</a> 30 in <a href="/wiki/Porto_Alegre" title="Porto Alegre">Porto Alegre</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-120" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-120">&#91;120&#93;</a></sup> In the last 16 against <a href="/wiki/Nigeria_national_football_team" title="Nigeria national football team">Nigeria</a>, his pressure led to <a href="/wiki/Joseph_Yobo" title="Joseph Yobo">Joseph Yobo</a> scoring a late own goal for a 20 French victory.<sup id="cite_ref-121" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-121">&#91;121&#93;</a></sup> France were eliminated in the quarter-finals by eventual champions Germany.<sup id="cite_ref-122" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-122">&#91;122&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Euro_2016">Euro 2016</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Antoine_Griezmann&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Euro 2016">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Suisse_-_France_2016_-_Griezmann_(crop).png" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/44/Suisse_-_France_2016_-_Griezmann_%28crop%29.png/170px-Suisse_-_France_2016_-_Griezmann_%28crop%29.png" decoding="async" width="170" height="207" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/4/44/Suisse_-_France_2016_-_Griezmann_%28crop%29.png 1.5x" data-file-width="250" data-file-height="304" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Suisse_-_France_2016_-_Griezmann_(crop).png" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Griezmann playing against Switzerland at <a href="/wiki/Euro_2016" class="mw-redirect" title="Euro 2016">Euro 2016</a></div></div></div>
<p>Griezmann was chosen for France as they hosted <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2016" title="UEFA Euro 2016">UEFA Euro 2016</a>, and started the opening game, a 21 win over <a href="/wiki/Romania_national_football_team" title="Romania national football team">Romania</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-123" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-123">&#91;123&#93;</a></sup> For their performances, he and <a href="/wiki/Paul_Pogba" title="Paul Pogba">Paul Pogba</a> were benched for the next game against <a href="/wiki/Albania_national_football_team" title="Albania national football team">Albania</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Stade_V%C3%A9lodrome" title="Stade Vélodrome">Stade Vélodrome</a>; Griezmann came on in place of Giroud in the second half and headed <a href="/wiki/Adil_Rami" title="Adil Rami">Adil Rami</a>'s cross with the first shot on target in the last minute to open a 20 win.<sup id="cite_ref-124" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-124">&#91;124&#93;</a></sup> In the last 16 against the <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Ireland_national_football_team" title="Republic of Ireland national football team">Republic of Ireland</a> in <a href="/wiki/Lyon" title="Lyon">Lyon</a>, he scored twice as the French recovered from a half-time deficit to win 21, and was also fouled by <a href="/wiki/Shane_Duffy" title="Shane Duffy">Shane Duffy</a> who was given a straight <a href="/wiki/Fouls_and_misconduct_(association_football)#Red_card_(dismissal)" title="Fouls and misconduct (association football)">red card</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-125" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-125">&#91;125&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 3 July, Griezmann assisted Pogba and <a href="/wiki/Dimitri_Payet" title="Dimitri Payet">Dimitri Payet</a> before scoring himself in a 52 quarter-final win over <a href="/wiki/Iceland_national_football_team" title="Iceland national football team">Iceland</a>; it was his first goal at the Stade de France.<sup id="cite_ref-126" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-126">&#91;126&#93;</a></sup> In the semi-finals against the country of his father's birth, Germany, four days later, he scored twice in a 20 victory to lead France to their third European Championship final.<sup id="cite_ref-127" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-127">&#91;127&#93;</a></sup> Following a 10 defeat to Portugal in the final on 10 July, Griezmann won the <a href="/wiki/List_of_UEFA_European_Championship_goalscorers#Top_scorers_by_tournament" title="List of UEFA European Championship goalscorers">Golden Boot</a> as the tournament's top scorer, with six goals and two assists in seven games, and was named the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2016#Awards" title="UEFA Euro 2016">tournament's best player</a>, also being named to the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_European_Championship_Teams_of_the_Tournament" class="mw-redirect" title="UEFA European Championship Teams of the Tournament">team of the tournament</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-best-player_128-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-best-player-128">&#91;128&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Golden_Boot_129-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Golden_Boot-129">&#91;129&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-tott_130-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-tott-130">&#91;130&#93;</a></sup> His tally of six goals at the tournament was second only to the nine goals by compatriot <a href="/wiki/Michel_Platini" title="Michel Platini">Michel Platini</a> at <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_1984" title="UEFA Euro 1984">UEFA Euro 1984</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Golden_Boot_129-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Golden_Boot-129">&#91;129&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="2018_World_Cup">2018 World Cup</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Antoine_Griezmann&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: 2018 World Cup">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>On 17 May 2018, Griezmann was called up to the France squad for the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018 FIFA World Cup</a> in Russia.<sup id="cite_ref-131" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-131">&#91;131&#93;</a></sup> On 16 June 2018, he suffered a foul in the box and scored the resulting <a href="/wiki/Penalty_kick_(association_football)" title="Penalty kick (association football)">penalty kick</a> to open the score in France's 21 over <a href="/wiki/Australia_national_soccer_team" title="Australia national soccer team">Australia</a> in their opening match at the tournament, which was the first penalty decision ever to be awarded in a World Cup match with the assistance of the <a href="/wiki/Video_assistant_referee" title="Video assistant referee">video assistant referee</a> system.<sup id="cite_ref-132" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-132">&#91;132&#93;</a></sup> On 30 June, Griezmann scored a goal from the penalty kick given for a foul on <a href="/wiki/Kylian_Mbapp%C3%A9" title="Kylian Mbappé">Kylian Mbappé</a> in a 43 victory over <a href="/wiki/Argentina_national_football_team" title="Argentina national football team">Argentina</a> in their round of 16 match.<sup id="cite_ref-133" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-133">&#91;133&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:FRA-ARG_(17).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/45/FRA-ARG_%2817%29.jpg/220px-FRA-ARG_%2817%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="186" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/45/FRA-ARG_%2817%29.jpg/330px-FRA-ARG_%2817%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/45/FRA-ARG_%2817%29.jpg/440px-FRA-ARG_%2817%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1021" data-file-height="865" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:FRA-ARG_(17).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Griezmann (middle) plays against Argentina in the round-of-sixteen game at the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018 FIFA World Cup</a></div></div></div>
<p>In France's 20 victory over <a href="/wiki/Uruguay_national_football_team" title="Uruguay national football team">Uruguay</a> in quarter-finals of the tournament on 6 July, Griezmann first assisted <a href="/wiki/Rapha%C3%ABl_Varane" title="Raphaël Varane">Raphaël Varane</a>'s goal from a corner and later scored a goal himself with a strike from outside the area following an error by Uruguayan goalkeeper <a href="/wiki/Fernando_Muslera" title="Fernando Muslera">Fernando Muslera</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-134" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-134">&#91;134&#93;</a></sup> Griezmann <a href="/wiki/Goal_celebration#Notable_non-celebrations" title="Goal celebration">did not celebrate his goal</a> against Uruguay out of respect for his Uruguayan mentor and Uruguayan club teammates.<sup id="cite_ref-135" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-135">&#91;135&#93;</a></sup> In the semi-final against <a href="/wiki/Belgium_national_football_team" title="Belgium national football team">Belgium</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Krestovsky_Stadium" title="Krestovsky Stadium">Krestovsky Stadium</a>, Saint Petersburg on 10 July, he set up the only goal of the game from a corner, which was headed in by <a href="/wiki/Samuel_Umtiti" title="Samuel Umtiti">Samuel Umtiti</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-136" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-136">&#91;136&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 15 July, Griezmann was involved in several goals in the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_Final" title="2018 FIFA World Cup Final">final</a> against <a href="/wiki/Croatia_national_football_team" title="Croatia national football team">Croatia</a>, which France won 42.<sup id="cite_ref-137" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-137">&#91;137&#93;</a></sup> With the score at 00 in the first half, France was awarded a foul on Griezmann after a challenge from <a href="/wiki/Marcelo_Brozovi%C4%87" title="Marcelo Brozovi">Marcelo Brozovi</a>. Commentators called that Griezmann had dived as he began falling before Brozovi made contact.<sup id="cite_ref-138" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-138">&#91;138&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-139" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-139">&#91;139&#93;</a></sup> Griezmann took the ensuing 30-yard (27&#160;m) free kick, which was headed by <a href="/wiki/Mario_Mand%C5%BEuki%C4%87" title="Mario Manduki">Mario Manduki</a> into his own net to give France the lead in the 18th minute.<sup id="cite_ref-Guardian-Summary_140-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Guardian-Summary-140">&#91;140&#93;</a></sup> Croatia equalized, but Griezmann scored a 38th-minute penalty after the referee ruled for handball (via a video assistant review) to give France a 21 lead.<sup id="cite_ref-141" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-141">&#91;141&#93;</a></sup> In the second half, he passed to <a href="/wiki/Paul_Pogba" title="Paul Pogba">Paul Pogba</a> in the build-up to the midfielder scoring the third goal for France.<sup id="cite_ref-142" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-142">&#91;142&#93;</a></sup> For his efforts, Griezmann was named man of the match,<sup id="cite_ref-MOTM_143-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MOTM-143">&#91;143&#93;</a></sup> and was also voted the third best player in the tournament behind <a href="/wiki/Luka_Modri%C4%87" title="Luka Modri">Luka Modri</a> and <a href="/wiki/Eden_Hazard" title="Eden Hazard">Eden Hazard</a>, receiving the <a href="/wiki/FIFA_World_Cup_awards#Golden_Ball" title="FIFA World Cup awards">Bronze Ball</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-144" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-144">&#91;144&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2018.E2.80.9319_UEFA_Nations_League"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="201819_UEFA_Nations_League">201819 UEFA Nations League</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Antoine_Griezmann&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: 201819 UEFA Nations League">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>On <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_UEFA_Nations_League_A" title="201819 UEFA Nations League A">Matchday 3</a> of the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Nations_League" title="UEFA Nations League">UEFA Nations League</a>, Griezmann scored a second half brace as the world champions came from behind to beat <a href="/wiki/Germany_national_football_team" title="Germany national football team">Germany</a> 21 in <a href="/wiki/Paris" title="Paris">Paris</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-145" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-145">&#91;145&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Style_of_play">Style of play</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Antoine_Griezmann&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Style of play">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p><a href="/wiki/UEFA" title="UEFA">UEFA</a> chief technical officer <a href="/wiki/Ioan_Lupescu" title="Ioan Lupescu">Ioan Lupescu</a>, who led the panel of technical observers that named Griezmann as the best player of Euro 2016, said that he "works hard for his team and possesses technique, vision and quality finishing" and branded him "a threat in every game he played".<sup id="cite_ref-best-player_128-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-best-player-128">&#91;128&#93;</a></sup> A quick, modern, and versatile left-footed <a href="/wiki/Forward_(association_football)" title="Forward (association football)">forward</a>, with an eye for goal, Griezmann has been described as a "team player", and is capable of occupying several offensive positions in or behind the main attacking line, due to his technical skills, ability to drop deep and link-up play between the forwards and midfielders, or score many goals: he has been deployed as a main <a href="/wiki/Forward_(association_football)#Striker" title="Forward (association football)">striker</a>, in a central role as an <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Attacking_midfielder" title="Midfielder">attacking midfielder</a>, or as a <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Winger" title="Midfielder">winger</a>, on either flank.<sup id="cite_ref-146" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-146">&#91;146&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-147" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-147">&#91;147&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-148" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-148">&#91;148&#93;</a></sup> Griezmann is an accurate finisher with either foot from both inside and outside the area, and is also good in the air and accurate with his head, in spite of his relatively small stature.<sup id="cite_ref-Griezmann_shows_he_is_among_the_best_149-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Griezmann_shows_he_is_among_the_best-149">&#91;149&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In addition to his ability to score and create goals, he has also been praised for his work-rate, attacking movement, positional sense, and ability to interpret the game, which, combined with his pace, mobility and energy, enables him to make effective attacking runs to beat the defensive line.<sup id="cite_ref-Catalyst_150-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Catalyst-150">&#91;150&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-FourFourTwo_151-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FourFourTwo-151">&#91;151&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-152" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-152">&#91;152&#93;</a></sup> He has been noted by various sources as having a comparatively low rate of scoring from penalties.<sup id="cite_ref-100th_64-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-100th-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-153" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-153">&#91;153&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-154" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-154">&#91;154&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-155" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-155">&#91;155&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Outside_football">Outside football</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Antoine_Griezmann&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Outside football">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Personal_life">Personal life</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Antoine_Griezmann&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Personal life">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Since 2011, Griezmann has been in a relationship with Erika Choperena, a Spanish native of the <a href="/wiki/Basque_Country_(greater_region)" title="Basque Country (greater region)">Basque Country</a>. They got married on 15 June 2017.<sup id="cite_ref-156" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-156">&#91;156&#93;</a></sup> They had their first child, a daughter named Mia, on 8 April 2016.<sup id="cite_ref-157" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-157">&#91;157&#93;</a></sup> The couple's second child Amaro, named after Antoine's grandfather Amaro Lopes, was born on 8 April 2019 (thus the siblings share their birthday).<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (January 2020)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup> Griezmann is <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic" class="mw-redirect" title="Roman Catholic">Roman Catholic</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-158" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-158">&#91;158&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-159" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-159">&#91;159&#93;</a></sup>
