</p><p>Griezmann's sister Maud was a survivor of the siege of the <a href="/wiki/Bataclan_theatre" class="mw-redirect" title="Bataclan theatre">Bataclan theatre</a> in the <a href="/wiki/November_2015_Paris_attacks" title="November 2015 Paris attacks">November 2015 Paris attacks</a>, which took place as he was playing against <a href="/wiki/Germany_national_football_team" title="Germany national football team">Germany</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Stade_de_France" title="Stade de France">Stade de France</a>, which was also site of an explosion in the same attacks.<sup id="cite_ref-160" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-160">&#91;160&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-161" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-161">&#91;161&#93;</a></sup> She is studying to become his image rights manager, while his younger brother, Théo, plays for Sporting Mâcon, an amateur French club, and in 2015 he created the sportswear brand GZ Brand.<sup id="cite_ref-mais_10-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-mais-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-162" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-162">&#91;162&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 17 December 2017, Griezmann caused controversy by sharing a photo of himself dressed as a <a href="/wiki/Harlem_Globetrotter" class="mw-redirect" title="Harlem Globetrotter">Harlem Globetrotter</a> on his social media accounts; the outfit included <a href="/wiki/Blackface" title="Blackface">darkened skin</a> and an <a href="/wiki/Afro" title="Afro">afro</a> wig. After severe criticism, Griezmann swiftly deleted the posts and apologized.<sup id="cite_ref-163" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-163">&#91;163&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Since Griezmann's time with Real Sociedad, he developed a strong affection for the country of <a href="/wiki/Uruguay" title="Uruguay">Uruguay</a>. His love for the country can be traced back to Real Sociedad Technical Director <a href="/wiki/Mart%C3%ADn_Lasarte" title="Martín Lasarte">Martín Lasarte</a> and teammate <a href="/wiki/Carlos_Bueno" title="Carlos Bueno">Carlos Bueno</a>, who are both <a href="/wiki/Uruguayans" title="Uruguayans">Uruguayan</a>. Bueno has been quoted multiple occasions about the origins of Griezmann's love for Uruguay began stating, "With him I began watching games everyday, he became fond of Uruguay and watched all <a href="/wiki/Pe%C3%B1arol" title="Peñarol">Peñarol</a> matches."<sup id="cite_ref-164" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-164">&#91;164&#93;</a></sup> In the <a href="/wiki/FIFA_2018_World_Cup" class="mw-redirect" title="FIFA 2018 World Cup">FIFA 2018 World Cup</a>, Griezmann scored a goal that helped knock Uruguay out of the quarterfinal. Griezmann commented, "I did not want to celebrate on the pitch -- I am very happy, but also sad for my [Atletico] teammates. It was my first time against Uruguay, so there was plenty of emotion."<sup id="cite_ref-165" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-165">&#91;165&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Media_and_sponsorships">Media and sponsorships</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Antoine_Griezmann&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Media and sponsorships">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Griezmann has a sponsorship deal with German sportswear company <a href="/wiki/Puma_(brand)" title="Puma (brand)">Puma</a>, and has appeared in commercials for the company.<sup id="cite_ref-Puma_166-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Puma-166">&#91;166&#93;</a></sup> His Hotline Bling <a href="/wiki/Goal_celebration" title="Goal celebration">goal celebration</a> features in a 2016 Puma commercial.<sup id="cite_ref-Puma_166-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Puma-166">&#91;166&#93;</a></sup> Puma unveiled Griezmann's own custom made football boots, PUMA Future 18.1 "Grizi", in December 2017.<sup id="cite_ref-167" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-167">&#91;167&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Griezmann features in <a href="/wiki/EA_Sports" title="EA Sports">EA Sports</a>' <a href="/wiki/FIFA_(video_game_series)" title="FIFA (video game series)"><i>FIFA</i> video game series</a>: he appears on the cover of the French edition of <i><a href="/wiki/FIFA_16" title="FIFA 16">FIFA 16</a></i> alongside global cover star <a href="/wiki/Lionel_Messi" title="Lionel Messi">Lionel Messi</a>, having been selected for the role by public vote.<sup id="cite_ref-168" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-168">&#91;168&#93;</a></sup> Ahead of Euro 2016, Griezmann featured in advertisements for <a href="/wiki/Beats_Electronics" title="Beats Electronics">Beats Electronics</a> headphones, alongside <a href="/wiki/Harry_Kane" title="Harry Kane">Harry Kane</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mario_G%C3%B6tze" title="Mario Götze">Mario Götze</a> and <a href="/wiki/Cesc_F%C3%A0bregas" title="Cesc Fàbregas">Cesc Fàbregas</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-169" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-169">&#91;169&#93;</a></sup>  He has a dancemove named after him in the popular French novelty song "<a href="/wiki/Logobitombo_(Corde_%C3%A0_sauter)" title="Logobitombo (Corde à sauter)">Logobitombo (Corde à sauter)</a>".<sup id="cite_ref-170" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-170">&#91;170&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Griezmann is a brand ambassador for <a href="/wiki/Head_%26_Shoulders" title="Head &amp; Shoulders">Head &amp; Shoulders</a> shampoo and <a href="/wiki/Gillette" title="Gillette">Gillette</a>, and has featured in several football themed television commercials.<sup id="cite_ref-171" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-171">&#91;171&#93;</a></sup> In 2017 he became a global brand ambassador for Chinese mobile phone manufacturer <a href="/wiki/Huawei" title="Huawei">Huawei</a>, however in December 2020 Griezmann formally cut ties with the company, citing "strong suspicions that [Huawei] has contributed to the development of a Uighur alert thanks to facial recognition software".<sup id="cite_ref-172" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-172">&#91;172&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Grizi_Esport">Grizi Esport</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Antoine_Griezmann&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Grizi Esport">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In January 2020, Griezmann launched his own esports organisation, Grizi Esport.<sup id="cite_ref-173" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-173">&#91;173&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-174" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-174">&#91;174&#93;</a></sup> The organisation has acquired <i>Rainbow Six Siege</i>, <i>Fortnite</i>, and <i>FIFA</i> players.<sup id="cite_ref-175" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-175">&#91;175&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-176" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-176">&#91;176&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Career_statistics">Career statistics</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Antoine_Griezmann&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Career statistics">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Club">Club</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Antoine_Griezmann&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: Club">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
